One of the biggest things God spoke to me during my fast is that he isn\u2019t calling me to leave my corporate job to put my faith in social media or my business, but to put my faith in him in a new and more significant way. \\n\\nI want to give a major shout out to all of the entrepreneurs out there. In a world where everyone\u2019s a critic and people judge 1st and ask question later - deciding to take the step to start a business and bring a vision you saw in your head to reality in-spite of that says a lot about your courage, character, boldness, and resilience. As entrepreneurs we can get so focused on constantly elevating and perfecting our craft that we forget to appreciate how far we have come, so I want to encourage you to look around from time to time and appreciate the work you\u2019ve already done. \\n\\nI am beyond excited for this next chapter, but the book that God has written leading up to this is already enough for a lifetime of gratitude.
